[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During a libFuzzer session [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the harness invoked the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.expand` routine on a generated testcase. While attempting to create a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompressor input stream for Z-compressed data, the JVM heap was exhausted and an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space` was thrown.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer framework classified this as a low-severity security issue—resource [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenial-of-service[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m caused by unbounded memory allocation when loading [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLZW tables.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace pinpoints the failure in `LZWInputStream.initializeTables`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash originates from `ZCompressorInputStream` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich extends [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during calls to [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream`.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness instrumentation logs confirm that `Expander`, `ExpanderFuzzer`, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumerous compressor and IO classes were loaded and instrumented before the crash.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A Java reproducer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Crash_ffc606ca8d3c2820239ab2d725e567e23327b470.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe raw crashing input were generated for further inspection.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand the breadth and impact of this issue, review the following [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially the [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception constructor expecting an `int`.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
